Softball's A Witch

by HarknessHottie

Summary

At Westview University, Agatha Harkness reigns supreme as the sharp-tongued catcher and captain of the softball team. With a picture-perfect boyfriend, a demanding double major in energy engineering and physics, and a reputation as the queen bee of campus, she seems to have it all—at least on paper.

But everything shifts with the arrival of Rio Vidal, a brooding transfer student whose blistering fastball and botanical obsession make her both a softball asset and a walking disruption. Majoring in botany and minoring in physics, Rio prefers plants to people and chaos to conformity, especially when it means ruffling Agatha’s perfectly curated life.

What begins as rivalry on the field quickly spirals into something far more tangled beneath the surface.

Chapter 1: Chapter 1: Meet Cute(ish)

Agatha is never late to class—that is, until today. It’s the first day of classes, and she is going to be late. Her routine was perfect: shower, get dressed, make the bed, have coffee and a granola bar, and walk to her first class.

Except for her walk to her first class, Physics, which was interrupted. One second, she is walking up the stairs, and the next, she is scrambling to stop her searing hot coffee from flying to the floor and unintentionally spilling it back onto her chest.

A gasp slips past her lips first, and then a frustrated and angry groan follows, with a death glare at the person who caused the problem. Her white blouse is ruined. Wide, brown, only slightly apologetic eyes stare back at her, but - wow. She's still mad, but maybe not as mad now because this woman is gorgeous and stuns her for a few seconds. The woman is dressed in all black, head to toe, from her Converse sneakers to the black hoodie over her head. Whatever insult she was preparing to spit out slips right out of her mind.

Then those eyes turn a little more appreciative of her wet blouse, and the insult is on the tip of her tongue once more.

“Are you blind?” Agatha grits out, quickly pulling the wet material away from her skin and hoping it didn't leak down to her La Perla bra. Who can blame her for taking a look?

Apparently, the brunette can.

Chapter 2: Chapter 2: Physics Lab

Chapter Summary

Agatha and Rio join together for a crucial physics lab on thermodynamics, but what happens when the science isn't the only thing heating up?

Agatha has made a point of being ten minutes early ever since the first day of class. She sticks with her same seat which happens to pay off because the professor always looks at her a few steps through the door. His eyes jump down her body just hoping coffee is spilled on her again. Agatha forces a smile until he looks away then grimaces with an eye roll. Suddenly a coffee cup is placed in front of her and she looks up to see Rio watching her with a cocky smirk, sunglasses on top of her head and hair pulled back into a messy bun.

Capiche?” Rio is slightly stunned in awe of those words rolling off of Agatha’s tongue with such ease but she manages to nod her head in agreement. Trying to think of all the ways she can get her to say it again.

“You feel like scarring old women on other days?” Rio jabs back swiftly. It earns her a fierce glare that only serves to rile up the butterflies in her chest. Fortunately for the pitcher, Miss Heart is basically knocking on the window so Agatha rolls down the driver’s side window with a plastered smile. 

 

“Miss Heart, what are you still doing here?” Agatha asks with a bit of an edge in her tone but the older woman is none the wiser. 

 

“Hi girls! Just cleaning up after the game. People can make such a mess. I thought you two would be gone by now? Out celebrating and such.” The older woman says cheerily. 

 

“Oh, we’ve been celebrating.” Rio mumbles, softly, but not softly enough. Agatha whips her head around with a deadly glare that promises a punishment near death. Is it terrible Rio can’t wait to be on the other end of her wrath? 

 

“What’s that dear?” Miss Heart questions with a blissfully clueless smile. 

 

“We’ll be celebrating tonight.” Agatha reiterates as she flashes her smile back on the older woman. “Speaking of - we should get going.” Agatha and Rio bid the other woman goodbye and drive off toward the dorms. 

 

“You’re in trouble.” Agatha glares, half serious, half teasing. Rio rolls her eyes and lets a small twitch of a smirk cross her lips. She can’t wait.

Chapter 18: Chapter 18: Poison Apples

Chapter Summary

Evanora is a bitch - are we surprised? Agatha isn't.

Rio and Agatha part ways before regrouping with the rest of the team for the many parties they will attend tonight. Being back in the dorm room isn’t exactly what Rio wanted out of the whole ‘weed debacle’ but it was part of getting her scholarship reinstated so she moved some of her things back in. While also keeping a few things at Agatha’s apartment, of course. The brunette had offered her apartment regardless of the woman getting her old dorm room back but they decided not moving in together after only three months was probably a smart choice. Right?

 

Agatha is starting to regret that decision when she opens the door, expecting Rio, only to find her Mother. Her blood runs cold and her stomach twists with that fun tug of anxiety and fear only Evanora Harkness can revoke. 

 

“Mother? What are you doing here?” Agatha asks, still trying to process the older woman’s sudden arrival. 

 

“Lovely to see you too, darling daughter of mine.” Evanora greets, swiftly side stepping her daughter to enter the apartment. Agatha’s face twists in complete confusion. Darling daughter of mine? Who the fuck says that? Certainly not Evanora Harkness. Agatha shuts the door, maybe a little harder than she intends, and faces her mother with arms crossed protectively over her chest. Whatever Evanora is here for, it isn’t good. 

 

It never is, now that Agatha is thinking about it. 

 

“Normally people call before showing up on someone’s doorstep.” Agatha responds tightly. Evanora looks around the apartment with disdain, even though Rio has made it her personal mission to keep the studio clean, and has been successful so far, the disgust is still bright in her cold blue eyes.

Rio’s sweatshirt, one that Agatha decidedly stole once she found out her girlfriend’s scent was ingrained into the material.The sweatshirt is light grey with blood red lettering across the chest of the clothing. The one that reads ‘Eastview Community College’. Yeah, that one, which she so casually tossed over the back of the couch earlier. Pretty fucking hard to miss.

“You have something to tell me.” Evanora doesn’t pose it as a question, it’s a statement. Agatha schools her features back into practiced neutrality.

Like an eagle, the older woman starts cataloging every single item that so clearly doesn’t belong to her daughter.

 

Rio’s green boxers. A green flannel. More Eastview spiritwear. A botany textbook. 

 

A fucking plant for christ sake. 

 

A small plant but a green one that Agatha hasn’t killed with her black thumb yet. Agatha can’t even remember the name of it. Only that Rio looked so damn adorable carrying it into the apartment with that huge smile on her face. Agatha remembers kissing her because of it. 

 

It feels like Evanora is looking into her memories when she turns back to Agatha with a piercing look, knowing and devastating. 

 

“It wasn’t a question, dear.” Evanora states firmly, moving closer and snagging the eastview sweatshirt off the back of the couch as she stalks closer. Fuck. She thrusts the sweatshirt into Agatha’s arms and raises an eyebrow.

“Tell you wh-”

 

“Don’t even think about trying to get out of this, Agatha Harkness. I know everything.” Evanora may as well have slapped her with the amount of venom behind her words. Agatha looks away but suddenly her mother has a grip on her jaw, squeezing her cheeks with pointed nails and jerking mirrored blue eyes back to her own. Agatha feels a rush of fear flood down her spine like ice water but she doesn’t have the heart to back down. 

 

“Sounds like you have your suspicions. Take a guess.” Agatha grits out through clenched teeth, daring the older woman to speak her thoughts into existence. 

 

“Pathetic.” Evanora hisses, releasing her daughter’s face with a rough shove and shaking her head in disgust. “If you’re going to disgrace the Harkness name at least take responsibility. You’re lucky I found out when I did. You could’ve destroyed the life I built for you” She shakes her head, waving her off with a scoff. Agatha tosses the sweatshirt onto the couch with a fierce glare and anger brewing in her chest. 

 

“Lucky? Th-The life you built? Are you joking? I-” Agatha’s anger rises alongside her voice, cutting herself off with a sudden boldness, raising her chin in defiance when her mother’s glare lands on her once again.

You really don’t want to know what’s in the bedroom.” Agatha laughs, knowing for a fact that their box of toys would give her mother a heart attack. On second thought…

 

“You are truly an imbecile,” Evanora hisses, “Do you have any idea what this kind of scandal would do to our family-” 

 

“Don’t make me laugh, mother. You’re worried about the company - nothing more, nothing less. Certainly not me, your own daughter - my happiness. Please.” Agatha cuts her off, refusing to hear the lie. Evanora laughs, fucking laughs, right in her face as an evil smile stretches across her lips. 

 

“The company- My company, is what gives you the life you have and I will be damned if you squander it with these impuissant feelings of happiness.” Evanora comes to stand within inches of her daughter, blue eyes staring like daggers into the clone of them. “Harkness Energy is your future. Success is your future. Happiness, your feelings, and the pathetic company you decide to keep is nothing but a road block keeping you from what you were made for.” Evanora spits, disgust and disappointment clear and present in every word.

 

Made for. Ever since she was born Agatha knew her one and only purpose in her mother’s eyes was to take over the family business. Except Agatha didn’t turn into the mini-Evanora the woman had hoped for. Instead, she became the exact opposite, and drove Evanora mad every day thereafter. Agatha feels her blood boil, fury and defiance rising like a tidal wave, ready to crash down on her with a destructive wrath.

 

“I’ll be sure to remind you of that when I destroy your precious little bartender under my heel.” Evanora speaks the words so smoothly, so soft, but just as cutting. Agatha’s bravado crumples under the weight of her mother’s words, heart dropping into her stomach like a brick. The tidal wave of anger inside of her dissipates in seconds. 

 

“What?” She utters softly, brow furrowing in confusion and concern as her gut once again twists with fear. 

 

“I’m not an idiot, Agatha.” Evanora sighs with a shake of her head, perpetually disappointed by her daughter. She crosses her arms and studies her daughter with a sharp gaze. 

 

“You are stubborn, something you got from me, unfortunately. Though it seems like it may be the only trait you inherited.” Evanora huffs. “Either way, I won’t get anywhere with you but your friend…” Evanora chuckles lightly, enjoying the way her daughter’s face drops at the implication.

 

“Oh, yes. Your precious Rio will be nothing once I am done with her. No scholarship, no team, no future. I may even debate taking her home if you make things especially difficult for me.” The older woman begins examining her manicure as if making threats is just another Tuesday. Maybe it is. 

 

“No,” Agatha states strongly, tries to at least, but her voice waivers with emotion. Would she follow through? Would Evanora take everything Rio has worked so hard for - and more? “Yes.” Evanora hissed, light flying in her eyes at the defiance, “I won’t let my daughter, the heiress to the Harkness fortune, become anything but a woman of power.”

“I don’t want to hurt the poor girl. Not to the media.” Evanora begins stalking closer, a deadly gleam in her eye, “She will be labeled a drug dealer who grows weed in her dorm room provided by the state through her scholarship. Agatha might be sick.

Agatha swallows the fear and panic in her throat. “You know about that?” Agatha whispers, trying hard to hide how much her voice shakes. 

 

“Stark has been on my well endowed payroll long before you came into the picture. Did you really think he was keeping your little secrets?” Evanora raises an eyebrow. Agatha’s jaw clenches and she feels pain zip through her from the tightness of her muscles. A headache begins crawling up her brain stem. Agatha closes her eyes and pinches the bridge of her nose, breathing deeply. 

 

“What do you want me to do, Mother?” Her voice is nothing but a strained whisper. 

 

“Dump her.” Evanora says simply, glancing down to admire her perfectly manicured nails once again as if she is becoming bored with the conversation, meeting her daughter’s incredulous blue eyes with a stern look.

“You heard me.”

Because that is all she is to her mother - a failure. She snaps her jaw closed, clenching her teeth together and willing the tears away. She knows what is coming.

When she comes up with nothing she has no choice but to plan for the alternative.

That must be where her mother’s heart is - the abyss.

Hanging off of Ralph’s arm.

Agatha doesn’t deserve her.

The drive to their three story, old-world charm, brick and mortar townhouse was not far from Harkness Energy headquarters. It took a while to find a home that matched them both but as soon as they saw this one they put in a cash offer. 

 

On the first floor, Agatha got the best of her dream in a home library. A mahogany-paneled study with floor-to-ceiling shelves, filled with rare grimoires alongside corporate contracts and scientific journals. A few botany books from Rio’s collection have drifted in from the living room. A heavy desk faces the fireplace, where Agatha often strategizes late into the night.

 

The kitchen was Rio’s domain. A blend of modern and old-world charm. Exposed brick walls, brass fixtures, and marble counters. Rio’s influence shows in the indoor herb garden, growing everything from basil to foxglove under soft grow-lamps. 

 

Agatha’s touch came through the woodwork of the walls in how she decorated the space for her wife, elegantly themed kitchen towels and a cheeky themed apron with ‘kiss the cook’ scrawled across the chest. 

 

Nicky thought it was hilarious. He would call Agatha into the kitchen just to point out the obvious rule as soon as his other mother adorned the apron. Rio would simply smirk in a mix of mischief and amusement, refusing to reject the boy's obvious truth. 

 

More often than not, Agatha would have to tell him she couldn’t kiss Momma the entire time she cooked. But she indulged in a few pecks with her wife before ushering her son, who inherited her bad trait as a cook from her, into the family room. The front room was softer, cozier—Nicholas’ toys tucked in wicker baskets, walls lined with framed photos of milestones, travels, and family mischief. 

 

They love this house. 

 

Rio turns the key and opens the door to let Agatha step through first. When she isn’t immediately hit with a little body in her knees she glances back at Rio who shuts the door. It’s late in the night but their son has a habit of pretending to sleep until he can see her, running down the stairs and into her legs as soon as she steps through the door. 

 

“Lilia offered to take him for the night,” Rio answers knowingly, she spots the sudden drop of a frown on her wife’s features and moves closer. “He’ll be back first thing in the morning to make sure his bags are packed for the trip. Don’t worry.”  Rio takes Agatha’s purse and drops down to one knee to take off the heels on her wife’s feet. 

 

“Oh, that was nice of her.” Agatha mutters. She would’ve liked to see him but having an uninterrupted night with her wife is hard to be upset about. She places a steadying hand on a strong shoulder as she steps out of the heels aching her feet. She flexes them against the weathered hardwood of the townhome and sighs. Rio stands, placing the purse on its hook and taking the brunette’s hand to lead her upstairs. 

 

“Nicky will be thrilled to see you in the morning, mi amour,” Rio says sincerely, tugging Agatha along, “He’s raving about dinosaurs right now. I’m sure he’s sweet talked Lilia into buying him more so I’m sure we’ll get a haul.” She explains with a fond smile, using the word Nicky learned from his Aunt Jen. 

 

Agatha always says Nicky inherited Rio’s charm. It only proves to be true when anyone in his life seems to eat up all the cuteness he uses to bargain for anything he wants - and gets. 

 

“Get undressed, baby, I’ll run the bath.” Rio leaves the brunette in the middle of the large primary suite as she walks into the large bathroom. One thing they both agreed on, a large, deep, clawfoot bathtub. She adds a few essential oils, lavender and bergamot, and a shake of epsom salt Jen gifted them to help the ache that will surely riddle their bodies in the morning. 

 

“Getting in with me, love?” Agatha asks as Rio turns toward her. The raven haired woman seems at a loss for words as her eyes skate down the brunette’s naked form. Rio takes a seat on the edge of the tub, spreading her legs to make room for the other woman as she slinks forward. 

 

“In a few minutes.” Rio reaches out to bring Agatha forward and runs her hands over her chilled skin. Agatha smiles and reaches behind Rio to pull her hair from the bun. 

 

“Good, don’t leave me waiting.” Agatha says playfully, leading Rio to look up at her as she leans down for a kiss. Rio smiles and leaves the bathroom on a mission. First she undresses, pulling on Agatha’s floral silk robe before walking down to the kitchen. When she returns back to the bathroom she has two water bottles in hand and a plate of snacks curated specifically to her wife. 

 

Agatha opens her eyes and raises an eyebrow, “Am I getting the princess treatment for a reason?” She teases, lifting herself up to take the offered water bottle. 

 

Rio scoffs, “Pft, please. You get Queen treatment all year round and you know it.” She teases back, setting down the other items on the stand beside the tub before removing the robe and settling in behind her wife. She sighs, leading Agatha to lean back against her as her left arm wraps around her middle. 

 

“That I do, wife.” Agatha agrees contentedly, dropping her head back to a strong shoulder and closing her eyes once more. They sit in comfortable silence. The hot bathwater begins to quell the aches in their bones. Rio sits behind her, fingers sifting through Agatha’s hair and all energy is lost. They’re not as young as they once were. 

 

“Take me to bed?” Agatha asks sleepily, rolling her head towards Rio’s to place a kiss on her cheek. Rio smiles and nods her head. Soon enough they are climbing into bed and wrapped in each other’s arms. They don’t even remember when they fell asleep, only that a collection of flying elbows and knees wake them up. 

 

“Oh, good lord.” Agatha groans, an elbow in her ribs and a knee in her thigh, eyes peaking open to see Nicky smiling brightly on top of them where Rio currently spoons her in their bed. Rio makes a similar groan of pain. 

 

“Coño, mi hijo.” Rio hisses, also cracking open her eyes to see their son, “I caught an elbow to the chest and a knee to the ass.” Nicky giggles and Agatha can’t help the smile from spreading across her face as well. Lilia must’ve dropped him off and let him through the door before bailing. 

 

“What did we say about flying limbs, sweet boy?” Agatha asks. Nicky giggles some more and hides his face in Rio’s arm. Another smile joins the party. Rio swiftly puts some space between herself and Agatha then drags the little boy between him. 

 

“Gonna answer Momma or do I have to tickle it outta ya?” Rio threatens with a slight narrow of her eyes. A squeal of excited fear screeches from the little boy. 

 

“No! Mami, no! Please!” Nicky cries out. Agatha spins around in the bed and prepares herself. Rio gives her a nod and they attack. The boy wiggles like a worm between them, shrieking and begging for the tickles to stop. Nicky finally apologizes and they retreat from the attack. 

 

“How did you sleep, honey? Did you get some rest?” Agatha asks, brushing his wild, curly brown hair from his eyes. The little boy huffs out a breath but smiles with a sure nod. 

 

“Yes, Momma. I got a new dinosaur from aunt Lilia, ate some ice cream, then fell asleep sooo hard in my dinosaur bed.” Nicky explains happily. Rio pops her head up over the boy with a smug smile. Agatha rolls her eyes and shakes her head. 

 

“Of course she did.” Agatha laughs lightly, pulling Nicky closer to place a resounding kiss on his cheek. 

 

“Are you ready for the trip mi hijo?” Rio questions curiously, knowing full and well that the little boy has been looking forward to this trip for weeks. Nicky suddenly shoots out of bed, throwing even more elbows and knees as he climbs over his mothers. 

 

Rio groans in pain, “How does such a small boy have such a lethal body?” She sighs and reaches back over to pull Agatha into her arms. The brunette smiles and curls into her wife, enjoying the warmth. “Abuelita would’ve fattened him up years ago.” She whispers. 

 

Agatha honest to god snorts, “I have no doubt she would’ve kidnapped him just to put some meat on his bones.” Rio chuckles and wraps her wife tighter. They last all of five minutes in blissful peace when their son runs back into their room. 

 

“Momma! Mami! Come on,” The little boy dramatizes the words as he climbs back on the bed, slower and not throwing limbs this time. He flops on top of them regardless. “Aunty Alice and Aunty Jen are gonna get there before us. We have to leave, like right now.” He gushes, a signature pout forming on his lips with an over exaggerated bottom lip. Agatha rolls her eyes and Rio chuckles. Exactly like his Mami. 

 

“Okay, okay. We’re getting up.” Agatha drags herself out of bed then Nicky and finally Rio. It doesn’t take long to load their bags and get Nicky settled into the Escalade out front, soon enough they’re on their way to Salem, Massachusetts to meet Alice, Jen, Lilia and Mrs.Hart.

 

They pull up to the cabin, the castle of cabins according to Nicky, when it is truthfully only a three bedroom two bath cabin at the edge of a lake but Nicky adores it. They bought it not long after Nicky started walking and connecting with anything outside - grass, dirt, flowers, anything under the sun. Soon, cabin trips in the fall were their favorites and a few family friends decided to tag along. 

 

Alice and Jen bought their own cabin, then Lilia began tagging along and eventually got her own. It’s been two years since their last trip and Nicky is thrilled. He’s nearly buzzing in his seat as the back door opens and Rio helps him out of the Escalade. 

 

“Be careful Nicky!” Agatha calls out quickly, pushing her sunglasses to the top of her head to watch him run off toward the cabin. Rio chuckles and begins grabbing their bags from the trunk. 

 

“He’s going to drive you nuts this week,” Rio teases, hoisting a bag onto her shoulder and then another. They have a lot of bags. Shocker. Agatha and Nicky travel with a minimum of two bags meanwhile Rio could live out of a single duffle for the week. Which she is. 

 

“I just wished he got my caution,” Agatha grumbles with a frown before spinning on her wife, “Instead he got your reckless, caution to the wind, fly by the seat of his pants attitude from you.” 

 

Rio smirks and shifts the bags higher onto her shoulder, “I thought you loved that about me, mi esposa.” She flirts shamelessly as she steps closer to her wife. Agatha smiles and accepts the advance by using one hand on Rio’s jaw to press their lips together. 

 

“I do love that,” Agatha husks, her fingers scratching lightly at Rio’s jaw, “About you. Not our son.” Rio hums softly in agreement. Agatha gives in to one more kiss and begins walking to the cabin with nothing but her purse in hand.

 

“Uh, mi amour,” Rio grabs another bag from the car, “Are you gonna help-” 

 

“This is another thing I love about you, my love. You have the muscles in the family. I’ll see you inside." Agatha calls out over her shoulder before disappearing into the cabin. Rio huffs with a small smile but follows after her carrying their bags. 

 

Nicky keeps himself busy outside as Agatha unpacks their clothes and Rio cleans off the dust around the cabin. Alice and Jen show up with Lilia after a few hours pass. Luckily they come bearing pizzas and beers. After a few slices and a few hours to catch up, the sun starts to set and Nicky is begging for s’mores. 

 

“When was the last time you built a fire, Vidal?” Alice taunts as she brings over more firewood where the raven haired woman is struggling to set up the wood. Rio huffs and narrows her eyes at the other woman. Nicky copies the look from beside his mother, making Alice chuckle. 

 

“Zip it Wu. I don’t need to remind you what happened the last time you challenged my skills, do I?” Rio quips back with a cheeky smile. Alice glares and Lilia groans. 

 

“Please, no more fire starting competitions. I barely escaped with my life.” Lilia sighs with a shake of her head, sipping her wine with the delicate tip of her glass. 

 

Agatha snorts, “You? I caught on fire.” 

 

“That’s a little dramatic, Harkness,” Jen tries to defend her wife only to have a mischievous smirk cross her lips, “Alice put it out quickly.” Alice narrows her eyes at her wife but she can’t help the amused smile that comes across her lips. She tries to bite it back but Jen sees it and smiles wider. 

 

Rio chuckles and beckons her son closer, “Come here, Nicky.” Agatha is seconds from vetoing when she bites her tongue. She trusts her wife but she still watches anxiously. Rio leads him through the process and helps him with the spark. It takes a few tires but soon enough there are embers in the kindling. A few calculated blows of air has the fire catching and roaring with fuel. 

 

“Good job, mi hijo. Go sit with Momma.” Rio praises as she gives his cheek a kiss and urges him toward the brunette. Agatha smiles with a wink toward the other woman and pulls Nicky into her lap, wrapping him up in her blanket. 

 

“Was that fun, Nicky?” Agatha asks softly. 

 

Nicky smiles and nods his head, “I liked it a lot, Momma.” A fire glints in his eyes. Oh boy. They might have a little pyro on their hands. From a glance at her wife, she knows exactly where it comes from. Rio crouches and stands, adding wood to the fire then blowing gently to get the right pieces to light. She looks gorgeous tending to the fire. 

 

“Who’s in charge of the s’mores?” Lilia questions excitedly. It is no surprise when Nicky offers his services, scrambling from Agatha’s lap to run back to the cabin. Once everything is gathered, Agatha being the main s’mores builder, Rio helps Nicky roast the marshmallows over the fireplace. He insists everyone eats a s’more, forcing Jen’s refusal with his signature pout until she caves. Nicky is the last to get his s’more, rewarding himself with two, one in each hand, as he sits in Aunt Alice’s lap. 

 

They reminisce on their old college days and catch up with each other’s lives through the two years they’ve been spread across the country. Jen and Alice moved across the country to California to build Jen’s skincare company and expand Alice’s Private Investigator, Bodyguard, and Bounty Hunter business. Lilia moved north to upstate New York, running a small boutique and taking on a few high end clients as a part time therapist. 

 

The night begins running late and Nicky is curled into Rio’s chest now. She shifts the blanket over his sleeping form and runs a hand along his back. Agatha watches in adoration. She got what she wanted. The best of both worlds. Rio, the love of her life, and their son, Nicky, who is the light of their lives, all while running a multibillion dollar company. 

 

Suck it Evanora.
